NOTIFICATIONS  BY  GOVERNMENT
COMMERCIAL TAXES AND REGISTRATION
DEPARTMENT
Provision for the consolidation of duty chargeable in
respect of issue of fully compulsorily convertible
Debentures for M/s. Infrastructure Leasing and Financial
Services Limited by the IL & FS Tamil Nadu Power
Company Limited under the Indian Stamp Act.
[G.O. (Rt.) No. 34, Commercial Taxes and Registration (J1),
23rd January 2014, ¬î 10, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜
Ý‡´- 2045.]
No. II(2)/CTR/146/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by clause (b) of sub-section (1) of Section 9 of the Indian Stamp
Act, 1899 (Central Act II of 1899), the Governor of Tamil nadu
hereby provides for the consolidation of duty of Rs. 25,00,000
(Rupees Twenty five lakh only) chargeable under the said Act in
respect of issue of 3,52,000 Fully Compulsorily convertible
Debentures for a face value of Rs. 10,000/- each to
M/s. Infrastructure Leasing & Financial Services Limited by the
IL & FS Tamil Nadu Power Company Limited.
C. JAYARAMAN,
 Deputy Secretary to Government.
ENVIRONMENT  AND  FOREST  DEPARTMENT
Notifications under the Tamil Nadu Forest Act.
Declaration of Hullathi, Melur Nandhatty Forest Block in
Udhagamandalam Taluk, The Nilgiris District as
Reserved Forest under the Act.
[G.O. (Ms.) No. 205, Environment and Forests (FR.14),
20th December 2013, ñ£˜èN 5, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜
Ý‡´ 2044.]
No. II(2)/EF/147/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 16 of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882 (Tamil Nadu
Act V of 1882) the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby declares that
the area, the boundaries of which are specified in the Schedule
below, as reserved forest with effect on and from the
18th August 2014.
SCHEDULE
(1) Name of the District  :
The Nilgiris.
(2) Name of the Taluk    :
Udhagamandalam.
(3) Number and Name   :
No. 13, Kadanadu
of the Village
(Previously Number 2,
Kadanadu)
(4) Name of the Forest
Hullathi, Melur Nandhatty
Block
    :
Forest Block
(5) Survey Number of
the Forest Block     :
Revised Survey No. 405/4
(6) Extent of the Forest
Block
              :
200.53.0 Hectares.
BOUNDARIES.
North:—Starting from the trijunction of the Village Number
12, Hullathi Village  and survey field Number I and 405/4 of
Village Number 13, Kadanadu Village the boundary generally
runs eastwards passes along the southern side of the field
number I and meet at the trijunction point of survey field number
1,401 and 405/4 all of the Village number 13, kadanadu Village.
East.—Thence, the boundary runs southwards passing
along the western side of Survey Field Numbers 401, 402 and
403 and meet at the junction point of survey field Numbers 403,
404, 5 and 405/4.  Thence, the boundary runs westwards,
southwards, eastwards, northwards and eastwards along the
northern, western, southern and eastern side of Survey Field
Number 404 and meat at the trijunction point survey field
Numbers 404, 5 and 405/4.  Thence, the boundary runs south
eastwards passes along the western side of field number of 5
and meet at the trijunction point of field  number of 5,399 and
405/4 and then runs south-west wards passes along the western
side of Survey Field number 399 and meet at the trijunction
point of Survey Field Numbers 399, 400 and 405/4 and thence,
the boundary runs southwards and east wards along the west
and south side of Survey Field Number 400 and meet at the
trijunction point of Survey Field Number 400, 372, 405/4 then the
boundary runs southwards passes along the western side of
Survey Field Nos. 372, 373 and 375 and turn West wards
passes along the northern side of survey field number 375, 405/
6. 376, 377, 378 and meet at trijunction point of Survey Field
numbers 378, 419 and 405/4 all of Village number 13 Kadanad
Village.
South.—Thence, the boundary runs generally westwards
and southwards passes along the northern and western side of
Survey Field numbers 419, 420 and meet at the trijunction point
of Survey Field numbers 420, 427 and 405/4.  Thence, the
boundary generally turns south westwards along the northern
side of Survey Field  numbers 427, 428 and 431 and meet at
the four junction point of Survey Field numbers 431, 461, 462
and 405/4 and the boundary line runs north westwards passes
along the northern side of the survey field numbers 462. Thence,
the boundary runs north eastwards and north westwards, along
the eastern and northern side of 405/5 and runs south west
wards along the northern side of Survey Filed Numbers 405/5,
464, 465 and 466 and turns southwards passes along the
western side of Survey Field numbers 466, 467, 470 and  turns
south westwards and passes along the northern side of the
Survey Field number 471 and meet at the trijunction of Survey
Field Numbers 471, 405/4 of No. 13, Kadanadu
Village and Village Number 12 of Hullathi Village.
West.—Thence, the boundary runds generally northwards
along the eastern side of Village number 12, Hullathi village and
then the boundary runs eastwards and northwards passes along
the south and east side of the Survey Field Number
405/2 and meet at the trijunction point o Survey Field Numbers
405/2, 405/4 of Village Number 13 Kadanadu Village and Village
Number 12, Hullathi Village. Thence, the boundary runs towards
north along the eastern side of Village Number 12, Hullalthi
Village and meet at the starting point.

Declaration of Moongilpatty Block-II in Natham Taluk,
Dindigul District as Reserved Forest under the Act.
[G.O. (Ms.) No. 208, Environment and Forests (FR.14),
26th December 2013, ñ£˜èN 11, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜
Ý‡´ 2044.]
No. II(2)/EF/148/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 16 of the Tamil Nadu Forest Act, 1882 (Tamil Nadu
Act V of of 1882) the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby declares
that the area, the boundaries of which are specified in the
Schedule below, as reserved forest with effect on and from
the 18th August 2014.
SCHEDULE
(1) Name of the District
:
Dindigul.
(2) Name of the Taluk
:
Natham.
(3) Number and Name of
the Village
:        No.23,Chellappa-
Naickenpatty
(Previously 39,
Chellappa-
Naickenpatty)
(4) Name of the Forest Block :
Moongilpatty,
Block-II
(5) Survey Number of the
Forest Block
       :
241/1
(6) Area of the Forest Block
:
30.29.55
Hectares.
BOUNDARIES.
North:- The boundary starts from the junction of Survey
Field Numbers 246, 240, 438 and 241/1 of Village Number.
23, Chellappanaickenpatty Village the boundary runs generally
towards east wards along the southern boundaries of survey
filed numbers 438, 229 (part) 241/2, again 229 (part) and
241/3, till it reaches the junction point of survey field numbers
241/3 and 241/1.  Thence this boundary turns towards north
and west wards and runs along the east and northern sides
of 241/3, till it reaches the quadra junction point survey field
numbers 229, 228, 241/1 and 241/3, of the said illage.  Thence,
it turns generally towards north wards and runs along the
eastern boundary of survey field number 228 till it reaches the
trijunction point of survey field numbers 241/1, 228 and
241/4 of the said Village and turns generally towards east wards
along south and eastern boundaries of survey field number
241/4 southern side of 225 and 224 and reaches the
trijunction point of survey field numbers 224, 221 and
241/1 of the said Village.
East.—Thence, the boundary generally turns towards south
wards and runs along the western side of survey field numbers
221, 220 and 217 of No. 23, Chellappanaikenpatti Village tilll
it reaches the trijunction point of survey field numbers
217, 242 and 241/1 of the said Village.
South.—Thence, the boundary generally turns towards west
wards and runs along the north, west, again northern side of
survey field number 242 and northern boundary of survey field
numbers 244, 245 OP No. 23, Chellappanaikenpatti Village till
it reaches the trijunction point of Survey Numbers
246, 245 and 241/1 of the said Village.
West.—Thence, the boundary runs generally towards west
and north wards along the eastern boundary of survey field
number 246 till it reaches the starting point.
Enclosures: The following fields are kept as enclousers
within the forest block:-

HOME DEPARTMENT
Constitution of one Special Court (in the cadre of
District Judge) and one Special Court (in the Cadre of
Sub Judge) to deal with MCOP cases at Dharmapuri
under the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act.
[G.O. Ms. No. 81, Home (Courts-II), 31st January 2014,
¬î 18, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2045.]
No. II(2)/HO/149/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by Section 3-A of the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act, 1873 (Central
Act III of 1873) the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consultation
with the High Court, Madras, hereby appoints one Additional
District Judge to the District Court, Dharmapuri for the purpose
of appointment as the member of the Motor Accidents Claims
Tribunal to be established at Dharmapuri and also fixes the
number of District Judge and Additional District Judges to be
appointed to the said Court as Four with effect on and from
the date on which the said Judge assumes charge of that
Court.
NOTIFICATION-II
[G.O. Ms. No. 81, Home (Courts-II), 31st January 2014,
¬î 18, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2045.]
No. II(2)/HO/150/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by the first paragraph of Section 4 of Tamil Nadu, Civil Courts
Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873) the Governor Tamil Nadu,
after consultation with the High Court, Madras, hereby alters
the number of Subordinate  Judges to be appointed under the
said Act for Dharmapuri District as Three with effect on and
from the date on which the Special Subordinate Judge, to deal
with Motor Accidents Claims Original Petition Cases assumes
charge of the Subordinate Judge’s Court at Dharmapuri.
NOTIFICATION-III
[G.O. Ms. No. 81, Home (Courts-II), 31st January 2014,
¬î 18, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2045.]
No. II(2)/HO/151/2014.—In exercise of the powers conferred
by 
second 
paragraph 
of 
Section 
4 
of 
the
Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act, 1873 (Central Act III of 1873),
the Governor of Tamil Nadu, after consultation with High
Court, Madras, hereby fixes the number of Subordinate
Judges to be appointed to the Subordinate Judge’s Court
at Dharmapuri in Dharmapuri District as Two with effect on
and from the date on which the Special Subordinate Judge,
to deal with Motor Accidents Claims Original Petition Cases
assumes charge of the that Court.
Notification-IV
[G.O. Ms. No. 81, Home (Courts-II), 31st January 2014,
¬î 18, Müò, F¼õœÀõ˜ Ý‡´-2045.]
No. II(2)/HO/152/2014.—In exercise of the powers
conferred by Section 10 of the Tamil Nadu Civil Courts Act,
1873 (Central Act III of 1873), the Governor of Tamil Nadu,
hereby fixes entire Dharmapuri District as the local limits
of the Jurisdiction of the Special Subordinate Judge’s Court
to deal with Motor Accidents Claims Original Petition Cases
of Dharmapuri.


Feb. 19, 2014]

Declaration of certain Traffic points cease to form Part of
the Local Areas of the Police Station in Certain Districts
under the code of Criminal Procedure.
Erode District
[G.O. Ms. No. 64, Home (Pol-XIV), 22nd January 2014.]
No. II(2)/HO/153/2014.—Under clause (s) of Section 2 of
the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1973 (Central Act 2 of 1974),
the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby declares that with effect
on and from the 22nd day of January 2014, the traffic points
specified in column (3) to the Schedule below, shall cease to
form part of the local area of the police stations specified in
column (2) thereof and shall form the local area of the police
stations specified in column (4) thereof:—

Withdrawal Notifications
[G.O. (4D) No. 1, Industries (MIG.2), 9th October 2013.]
No. II(2)/IND/155/2014.—Under sub-section (1) of Section
48 of the Land Acquisition Act 1894 (Central Act I of 1894)
the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby withdraws the acquisition
of land specified in the Schedule below in respect of which
Industries Department Notification No.II(2)IND/4351/92 published
at 
pages 
6 
and 
7 
of 
supplement 
to 
Part 
II
Section 2 of T.N.G.G. dated 9-9-1992 (Issued No. 36) Industries
Department. Notification No. II(2)/IND/2372/93 published at
Pages 6 and 7 of supplement to Part II section 2 of TNGG
dated 12-5-1993 (Issue No. 18C) and Industries Department
Notification No. II(2)/IND/3748/93, published at pages 8 and 9
supplement to Part II Section 2 of TNGG dated 4-8-1993 (Issue
No. 30A) under sub-section (1) of Section 4, Sections 6 and
7 of the said Act respectively as being required for a public
purpose to wit, for the setting up of an agro based Industrial
complex by Tamil Nadu Corporation for Industrial Infrastructure
Development Limited at Pallapatty Village, Nilakottai Taluk,
Dindigul District.
SCHEDULE
Dindigul District, Nilakottai Taluk, Pallapatti Village.
Government dry S.No. 222/2, belonging to Annathayammal,
bounded on the north by S.No. 223, east by S.No. 222/3, south
by S.o. 222/5 and west by S.No. 222/1—0.28.5 hectare.

AMENDMENTS TO NOTIFICATION
 [G.O.Ms. No. 274, Labour and Employment (J2),
22nd November 2013]
NO. II(2)/LE/158/2014.
In exercise of the powers conferred by Clause (a) of
sub-Section (1) of Section 5 read with Section 9 of the
Minimum Wages Act. 1948 (Central Act XI of 1948), the
Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby makes the following
amendments to the Labour and Employment Department
Notification No. II(2)/LE/239/2013, published on page 195
of Part II-Section 2 of the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette,
dated the 6th March 2013.
AMENDMENTS
In the said Notification.”—
(1) for the word “revision”, the word “fixation” shall
be substituted;
(2) under the heading “Independent Persons”.-
(a) In item  2, for the expression “Assistant
Commissioner of Labour Coimbatore”, the expression
“Assistant Commissioner of Labour-I (conciliation),
Coimbatore” shall be substituted;
(b) In item 3, for the expression “Assistant
Director, O/o the Director of Economics and Statistics,
Chennai-600 006”, the expression “The Assistant Director of
Statistics, Department of Economics and Statistics, No. 246,
N.S.R. Road, G.V.V. Complex, 2nd Floor, Venkittapuram,
Velardipalayam Post, Coimbatore-641 025” shall be
substituted.
Draft Notification regarding the Revision of minimum rates
of wages for employment in Carpentry  and Blacksmithy
under  the Act.
[G.O. (2D) No. 73, Labour and Employment (J1)
29th October 2013]
NO. II(2)/LE/159/2014.
The following draft of a Notification which it is proposed
to issue in exercise of the powers conferred by clause (b) of
sub-section (1) of Section 3 and sub-section (2) of
Section 5 of  the Minimum Wages Act, 1948 (Central Act
XI of 1948), is hereby published for information of all persons
likely to be affected thereby, as required by clause (b) of
sub-section (1) of Section 5 of the said Act.
2. Notice is hereby given that the draft Notification will
be taken into consideration on or after the expiry of two
months from the date of publication of this Notification in
the Tamil Nadu Government Gazette and that any objection
or suggestion, which may be received from any person with


Feb. 19, 2014]
TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE
225
respect thereto before the expiry of the aforesaid period, will
be considered by the Government of Tamil Nadu. Objection
or suggestion, if any, should be addressed to the Principal
Secretary to Government, Labour and Employment Department,
Secretariat, Chennai-600 009, through the Commissioner of
Labour, Chennai-600 006.

In exercise of the powers conferred by clause (b) of
sub-section (1) of Section 3 and sub-section (2) of Section
5 of the Minimum Wages Act, 1948 (Central Act XI of 1948)
and in supersession of the Labour and Employment

in Carpentry and Blacksmithy in the State of Tamil Nadu
specified in column (2) of the Schedule below, as specified
in the corresponding entries in column (3) thereof:-

Explanations:- 
(1) 
Classification 
of 
Zones:-
Zone A,B and C shall comprise of the following areas:-
Zone A: Corporations and Ambattur Municipality.
Zone B: All Municipalities except  Ambattur Municipality.
Zone C: Other areas.
(2) Dearness Allowance:- In addition to the minimum rates
of basic wages fixed above, the employees shall be paid
dearness allowance as indicated below:-
(i) The dearness allowance is linked to the Average
Chennai City Consumer Price Index for the year 2010, that
is 161 points (with base 2001=100) and for every rise of
one point over and above 161 Points, an increase of Rs.
47.25 (Rupees forty seven and twenty five  paise only) per
month shall be paid as dearness allowance.
(ii) The dearness allowance shall be calculated every
year on the 1st April of every year on the basis of the average
of the indices for the preceding twelve months, that is, from
January to December.
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 


226
TAMIL  NADU GOVERNMENT  GAZETTE
[Part II—Sec. 2
(iii) The first calculation shall be effective from the date
of publication of the Notification in the Tamil Nadu Government
Gazette, based on the Average Chennai City Consumer Price
Index Number for the previous year.
(3) Where the nature of work is the same, on distinction
in the payment of wages shall be made in the case of male
and Female Employees.
(4) To arrive at the daily rates of wages, the monthly wages
shall be divided by 26.
(5) To arrive at the monthly rates of wages, the daily rates
of wages shall be multiplied by 30.
(6) Wherever the existing wages are higher than the
minimum wages fixed herein, the existing wages shall be
continued to be paid.
MOHAN PYARE,
Principal Secretary to Government.
Disputes between Workmen and Managements referred
to Industrial Tribunal for Adjudication.

No.II(2)/SWNMP/203/2014.
In exercise of the powers conferred by sub-section (1) of
Section 29 of the Juvenile Justice (Care and Protection of
Children) Act, 2000 (Central Act 56 of 2000), the Governor of
Tamil Nadu hereby makes the following amendment to the
Social Welfare and Nutritious Meal Programme Department
Notification No. II(2)/SWNMP/297(b-4)2012. published at pages
2 
and 
3 
of 
Part 
II-Section 
2 
of 
the
Tamil Nadu Government Gazette, Extraordinary, dated the
11th June 2012.

624 302-Chairperson’’, the following expression shall be
substituted, namely:-

87/161, Gandhi Road,

Chairperson’’.
